    function goSearch(url) {
        if (url.includes("?")) {
            window.location.href = url + "&autoopencal=1";
        }
        else {
            window.location.href = url;

        }
    }

<script type="text/javascript">

    function subscribeNewsletter() {
        var newsletterEmailElement = document.getElementById('newsletter-email');
        var newsletterForm = document.getElementById('newsletter-form');

        var newsletterEmail = newsletterEmailElement.value;

        if (newsletterForm.classList.contains('has-success')) {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('POST', 'https://bluepillow-api.azurewebsites.net/newsletter/subscriptions');
            xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
            xhr.send('email=' + newsletterEmail + '&dontResendEmail=true');

            xhr.onload = function () {
                var newsletterFieldset = document.getElementById('newsletter-fieldset');
                newsletterFieldset.setAttribute('disabled', '');
            };
        }

    }

    (function () {
        var newsletterEmailElement = document.getElementById('newsletter-email');

        function validateEmail(e) {
            var emailErros = document.getElementById('email-errors');
            var noEmail = document.getElementById('no-email');
            var noValidEmail = document.getElementById('no-valid-email');
            var newsletterForm = document.getElementById('newsletter-form');

            var emailRegex = RegExp("^[a-zA-Z0-9.!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9](?:[a-zA-Z0-9-]{0,61}[a-zA-Z0-9])?(?:\.[a-zA-Z0-9](?:[a-zA-Z0-9-]{0,61}[a-zA-Z0-9])?)*$");

            var newsletterEmail = e.target.value;
            if (newsletterEmail === '') {
                // Error
                emailErros.style.display = '';
                noEmail.style.display = '';
                noValidEmail.style.display = 'none';
                newsletterForm.classList.add('has-error');
                newsletterForm.classList.remove('has-success');
                return;
            } else {
                emailErros.style.display = 'none';
                noEmail.style.display = 'none';
            }

            if (emailRegex.test(newsletterEmail) === false) {
                // Error
                emailErros.style.display = '';
                noEmail.style.display = 'none';
                noValidEmail.style.display = '';
                newsletterForm.classList.add('has-error');
                newsletterForm.classList.remove('has-success');
            } else {
                emailErros.style.display = 'none';
                noValidEmail.style.display = 'none';
                newsletterForm.classList.add('has-success');
                newsletterForm.classList.remove('has-error');
            }
        }

        newsletterEmailElement.addEventListener('input', validateEmail);
        newsletterEmailElement.addEventListener('propertychange', validateEmail);
    })();


</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function downloadJSAtOnload() {
        var lazyImages = document.querySelectorAll('.lazy-image')
        var inAdvance = 100

        function lazyLoad() {
            Array.prototype.forEach.call(lazyImages, function (image) {
                if (!image.classList.contains('loaded') && !image.classList.contains('loading-error')) {
                    var top = typeof image.getBoundingClientRect === 'function' ? image.getBoundingClientRect().top : image.offsetTop
                    if (top && top < (window.innerHeight + window.pageYOffset + inAdvance)) {
                        image.src = image.dataset.src
                        image.onload = function () { image.classList.add('loaded') }
                        image.onerror = function () { image.classList.add('loading-error'); image.src='/images/img-not-found.jpg' }
                    }
                }
            })
        }
        lazyLoad();
        window.addEventListener('scroll', lazyLoad)
        window.addEventListener('resize', lazyLoad)
    }
    if (window.addEventListener)
        window.addEventListener("load", downloadJSAtOnload, false);
    else if (window.attachEvent)
        window.attachEvent("onload", downloadJSAtOnload);
    else window.onload = downloadJSAtOnload;
</script>
